Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "contusion treatment," and it is that you make the patient who has this illness shave the hair from his forehead, then you make three incisions on the forehead equally according to its length;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and let one of the incisions be made in the middle of the forehead down to just above the nose, and the other two on either side above the eyes, and be careful not to cut into the arteries that are on either side above the eyes;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	and move your hand away from the connection of the two mandibles, and let each incision be the length of three fingers across the joint;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and prepare a piece of sponge and much cloth to wipe the blood, then place the spatula gently on both sides as shown in this form:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision that is near the temple to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and peel off all the skin that is between the two cuts to the surface of the bone, then do the same from the middle incision to the other second one, and then remove this spatula.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	Insert into the first groove the instrument called "cultellaire," and it is very well sharpened on one side, and on the other side it is smooth, not sharp, and this is its form:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the cutting edge towards the flesh of the heart, and the smooth side towards the bone, and insert it until it reaches the middle groove.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes so that the incision is continuous until it reaches the one that opens in the skin, and then do the same on the middle incision until you reach the other side.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	And then draw out the blood evenly, and press the area to expel the collected blood;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	Then place a piece of old cotton in each crevice, and apply cloths moistened with wine and oil and pitch, and guard against the formation of foul abscesses;
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And on the third day loosen the bandage, and apply a large poultice of boiled water, then treat it with basilicon ointment mixed with rose oil, and other treatments used for wounds, until he is healed.
dou reume des eulz	of the rheum of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone frequently suffers from acute catarrh, and you see the eyes swollen and small, with weakened vision, and the eyelids burned;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hair falls out, and on the head it causes severe pain like malaria, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	then you can tell from these symptoms that those matters and that catarrh come only from many veins, and if the physician treats what is there, this is correct.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you instruct the patient behind their forehead, then make a large incision across the forehead, and another at the back of the head.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	And start from the fissure of the left temple to the right temple, and let the incision go until it reaches the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that move during eating;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, wipe all the blood with a sponge, and then separate between the two lips of the fissure and place old cotton there, and bandage with linen;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then lay on top wet cloths in wine and oil, and guard against hot abscess;
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	When it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then treat with things that excite growth, which make flesh regenerate.
En teil maniere:	In such a manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of wheat flour, and four parts of colophony, and make a plaster;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	and apply it to these wounds to regenerate flesh throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the obstruction of the ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	All that falls into the ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	For seeds, for beasts, for stones from mines, or similar things such as iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	For seed, such as peas, beans, and lentils;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	For things that flow, such as water and pus and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When a stone or any other substance that does not fit into the ear and does not grow in the ear falls into it, place the ear towards the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, then drop a little bit of violet oil or cumin oil, then proceed with its removal;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and make them sneeze with spices, and plug the nostrils when the sneezing comes, and place around the ear pieces of cloth or wool;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and hold the ear above.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Much heat comes from this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not produce heat, then gently extract the pus with fine forceps, which is done as follows:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If it flows out freely with the forceps, that is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, then carefully extract it using a fine needle with a small incision;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if it does not flow out even then, make a thread of linen and insert the end of the thread into the ear canal firmly, and plug around the thread with soft wax so that no air can enter through the thread;
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then pull it out forcefully, as much heat often comes out as we have said;
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if it does not come out in such a manner, take the glue that birds use, and put some instrument that is sharp for this purpose, and place a little cotton around;
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	then press the glue on the stone or whatever it may be, and draw it out.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it does not come out from all the things we have said, then hurry to cut the ear as for an abscess so that the pus may flow, and relieve spasm;
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	and the manner of cutting is that you first let blood from the patient's head, and draw out blood according to the measure of his strength, then have the patient sit between your hands and turn the ear upwards, and make a small cut at the root of the ear into the fat or dependent area;
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and let the incision be as moon-shaped, until you reach the stone, then remove it according to your power, and suck it quickly into your mouth;
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue the treatment until he is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it is a grain that is inside and it swells, then administer extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot come out, then administer this salve thinly according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer an incision of that tumor.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not do this when you think the grain is moist due to moisture from the ear, until you have done this many times;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with fine forceps and with suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is gentle.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In acute cases where water enters the ear, the patient should use sneezing with pepper first, and plug the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And lie down on the side where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	if it comes out because of that, it is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	if not, take many stones according to the length of your thumb and light, and heat them a little in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and place them in the patient's ear one by one, and let them come out from under his foot on the other side, and press with another stone upon the stone that is in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and do not stop placing stone upon stone until the water completely exits, and thus it will all come out;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you wish, take some rush grass, and insert one end into the ear, and set fire to the other end until the softer part of the grass is burned;
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then perform another incision on other veins until all the fluid has drained out, as we have said regarding stones.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of the beast, if it is small, such as a flea or similar thing, treat it as we have said in the section.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if it is large enough to be felt, then treat with forceps for its extraction;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the easiest thing to remove that can be in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms from the ears, when you treat them as we have said in the section and in treating distillations, and if the treatment is ineffective, then you should examine the ear in sunlight:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If any worms are visible, remove them with fine forceps, and if none are seen, take the chain of which this is the form:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And insert the finer end into the ear according to the amount of pain felt by the patient, then proceed gradually with the chain.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this repeatedly until all the worms come out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not come out willingly, plug around the chain with cotton as I have said for stones;
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not exit as we have said, administer distillations that the ancients have used for worm expulsion, and you will find them in the treatment of distillations;
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and then pour your oils and medicines into the ear with all this equipment, as you see here in the form:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And whether it is of silver or brass, make it narrow with small holes, and place it above to let the liquid drip through;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to aid the dripping into the instrument made of brass for this purpose, if you wish, take a scraper and wrap it around the tip with cotton;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice, and whatever medicine you wish into the tube, and place the tube in the ear;
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then press into the scraper with all the cotton, and squeeze your hand gently until the oil drips down to the bottom of the ear;
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	and the patient feels it inside, and let the distilled liquid be heated over fire as one would distil it into the ear;
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	and ensure that it is not too cold, for the medicine would not be as good.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of the obstruction of the ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	Some children are born without any holes in their ears;
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	and this same thing happens to adults due to the closure of a wound, or from flesh grown inside the ear, and these obstructions sometimes occur deep in the ear, so that one cannot see them;
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and sometimes the liquid exits the hole clearly, and one can see it well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	The one that comes in deeply, if it cannot be seen, is a severe healing in many conditions, and for the one that can be seen, you should place the patient's ear towards the sun;
et regarde dedens:	and look inside:
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the ulcer clearly, then proceed with this treatment as described in this section:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	And let it be sharp and cutting in front and behind, so as not to touch the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the ulcer is of flesh from the ear, then hold it with fine forceps and scrape gently until all the tissue is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the wax is placed in the ear, take a fine razor and warm it slightly over the fire, then place it on the flesh of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you feel the waxiness where the patient feels pain in the ear, pierce gently, and be careful not to injure the nerves of the ear;
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	then place in the ear a tent according to the width of the opening, and apply the Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this for several days until the wound is sealed, then take a tent and apply it with rose water, and sprinkle powdered vitriol on top;
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and if you see the ear swollen, then it is necessary to remove the tent and apply another tent moistened in cerate made of rose oil and wax, until the swelling subsides;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him until he is healthy.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, plunge a sponge and cloths in cold water, and place it on the ear, and use other treatments that stop the bleeding which are in the treatment of hemorrhages.
de la char des papieres	of the flesh of papers
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This eyelid that comes in due to moisture and becomes dry, you should extend it with tweezers and forceps, and cut it from a spatula at its root;
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	then place vitriol powder over the area.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if there is no skin covering it, cauterize with a fine lentil-shaped cautery, and after the incision, apply a dressing.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and it often needs repair, as some of its roots remain.
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	and when they are cauterized with fire, those roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	from the hailstone
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Often come in the eyes things that resemble hail in form and hardness, and for this reason this disease is called "hailstorm," and it is a gathering of thick moisture above and below the eye.
li ovraiges est telz:	the work is such:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	take care if the hailstorm moves from one side to the other, and it is easy to know this.
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Then make an incision widely, then gently scrape each part, then take it with forceps, and remove it.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	if you cannot remove it without piercing the eye slightly, do not worry about harming the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	and if the wound is large, sew it up with stitches, and treat it until it heals;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	and if it is small, do not use force, for the ointment will heal it quickly and regenerate flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the grain is descending inside the ear towards the upper part, turn the paper over, and extract the grain with tweezers, and scoop and press from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	and if the paper is pushed away by the incision, it does not matter;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	and when the grain is removed, wash the eye with salt water, and treat the area that regenerates flesh until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	of the grease of the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a grease that forms on the threads of paper above, and this happens more often in children than in adults, and it greatly troubles their eyes, and they get catarrh in the mornings, and cannot look at the sunlight because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	and because of this they lie down immediately on their beds and sleep, and their papers under their eyebrows are moist, which swells and appears covered with the exinach that is apparent in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the area with your thumbs and feel the exinach between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of treatment is that the patient places their head in your lap;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	and then take a linen cloth, and prepare a tent in the shape of a circle according to the amount of exinach contained in each part, and place it over them;
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	And press on your two sides from both parts so that the extremity is assembled within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	Then make in the middle of the moisture with a sharp scalpel a narrow incision, and let it not be larger than the wound made when opening a vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	And cut through the skin deeply until you reach the extremity;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	And in many positions, the extremity comes from the incision, according to the form of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Extract it then in one piece with a torn cloth between your two hands from the outside, and turn your hand right and left until it is spread out;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And guard that you do not insert into the fissure, that you do not come to the entire socket up to the eye, that you do not injure it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the extraction does not begin at the start of the fissure, enlarge the fissure slightly until it begins.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract it as we have said, then moisten cloths with oil and water, and place them on the site, and bandage it.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And there are such people who grind salt and put it on to corrupt the moisture that remains.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him until he is well.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if he comes to the place of an abscess that is hot, treat him with soothing plasters until he is well.
des poilz des papieres	of the hair of the eyebrows
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow attached to areas other than where nature intended on the eyelids, and they are irritated, they harm the eyes and cause various diseases such as habitual tearing and inflammation of the eyelids and conjunctiva, until it becomes a reason for the destruction of the eyes;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment follows according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	or by cautery with fire altogether, or by medicine according to what is before in the chapter on cautery, and it is done either by incision and suturing or by canes, as I will say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary that you place the head of the patient in your lap, then turn the eye socket with your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it is turned, that is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, then insert a needle along the entire length of it;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and do this near the margin of the eye socket where the hair grows among the hairs, and pull the thread along the entire eye socket, and then turn it with a scraper;
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	Then make an incision on the part beneath the skin, between the attached hairs, covering the entire spatium, from the large joint to the small.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then extract the thread and place beneath the skin a small pad of cotton and linen, then apply over the skin a figure of incense, such as the leaf of myrtle, and whatever else is needed according to the amount you wish to lift the skin that is prescribed for all.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if there is need to cut away a great quantity of the skin according to how much the skin has softened;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then make the incision over the entire spatium along the two lines that you have marked, starting from the large joint to the small;
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	And let one of the incisions be near the natural hairs in the thickness of a root, then insert the lancet into one of the two corners of the wound, then scrape it all.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	Then sew the two lips together with a needle and fine linen thread, wipe away the blood, and apply a poultice of excess flax to both eyebrows with any sticky substances if you wish to do so.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	And if not, do not worry about it, then leave the stitches in for three or four days.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then treat the wound without stitches with drying and constricting substances, because the skin around the wound rises suddenly and comes together on its own, but stitching is slow (as the ancients say), and this work should be done without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	and there is another manner:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and it is that you cut the stone in a shape similar to the leaf of myrtle, as we have described, by three ounces separated according to the form which is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then cut those which rise above the smaller parts equally according to the shape which is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you are unable to hold the pliers and the pieces are not even, then take a needle with one thread, and place it in the opening;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and place one thread next to the large artery, and the second thread next to the small one, and tie them together equally;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin on which you have cut, as we have described, then stitch together the two edges of the wound, and treat it until it is healed;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	And if an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with plaster and similar soothing ointments;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	And sometimes the hair on the skin is turned back:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	It is necessary to use what we have said about incising;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the suturing in one case and the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of canes follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and it is that you turn the skin and make an incision according to what I have said, and then make two canes by hand, and two fine sutures as long as the skin and as wide as the spatula is;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and cut between two shoulders where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then carefully join one to the other above what protrudes from the eye's membrane, and pull apart the two tendons of each part firmly;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it like this for several days, and the skin which is pulled apart will die, become blackened, and pus up until it falls off on its own.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it delays, cut it with force, then treat it until it is healed;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and when the wound is closed, and if the membrane is raised, and the hairs will no longer prick;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of the two chains that you will make according to this figure, and according to this length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The work is such that you take a fine needle, and insert the thin silk thread underneath;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	then assemble the heads and tie them together finely, and let the length of the threads be one palm;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	then arrange another fine silk thread in the socket briefly, and tie the ends of the thread gently;
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	then have the patient place their head in your care;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	and place it near the sun so that the work is clearly visible, for this is delicate and intricate work; then insert the needle throughout the socket at the base of the hair adjacent to it, and pierce through the membrane quickly as you pull it over the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then remove the hair up to the wound, and insert that hair into the wound if there is one or two or three or more;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then withdraw your hand until the hair comes out completely from the wound along with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the wound is narrow and the hair does not come out with it, then draw the wound inward along the thread you have inserted until the wound comes out of the opening and you can see it with your eyes;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	then draw the wound and the thread out, and close the eye and leave it closed for two or three days until the hair hardens in its place and the flesh grows over.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are short, accompany it with a long hair from natural growth, and raise it alongside one you leave, until it is raised and then lift it.
de la porriture de l’oil	from the pus of the eye
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease called "aleacrati" or corruption comes to the eye, there are two ways it can occur:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	one naturally, and the other unnaturally.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens by sudden incision, or cutting, or cautery, and by similar things.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the method of treatment is that you cut open the closure, and separate the edges, and place linen tents inside, and keep it elevated until it heals;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	and it is not appropriate to use in the treatment of it things that dry out and constrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the illness will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but use things that soften it, such as fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and boil the dew of water and althaea seeds and flax seeds, then mix with some of the melted ointment, and wrap it in a cloth, and treat him with this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the goal of your treatment is to ensure that it does not heal in the same form as before;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	and the treatments we have mentioned are nothing but methods to prevent this illness from returning in its previous form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the flesh that comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease which is called "axacrati" in truth, and its nature and accidents.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The accident comes from a wound and a cut and a cautery and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the method of the procedure is that you take a needle, in which there is a double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make it pierce from the left tear duct to the right, so that the thread goes through two parts of the flesh;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then stretch the skin over the entire needle, and cut with a spatula that is one span wide.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the shape of the paper returns as it should, that is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	if not, then take a razor and place it in the cut, and turn the paper, and make two cuts on the side within the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the heads of the two grooves at the two corners of the incision you have made be such that when they are joined, the shape is like the letter called "I" in Greek;
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	then remove the flesh according to the sharpness of the angle inside, from where the paper was placed, then join the two separated parts together with a thread of wool;
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with the remedies we have mentioned for softening and stretching until he is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the illness comes from a wound or suture or cauterization, then you must make an incision cleanly between the hairs of the paper, as was described before;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then separate between the two leaves of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and the work should be done according to the form of the illness, for it is very diverse in form, and wise masters prepare their treatment with all their power to restore the figure to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and the patient himself, according to what is required of work and instruments in various conditions.
dou soudement de la papiere	of the sudden swelling of the skin
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this soldering occurs in some people in such a way that the paper above is soldered with the white of the eye, and cannot move or perform their natural tasks, then you should insert the point of a razor below the paper, and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	and hold the forceps, until you cut that which is attached to the fine spatula, which must not be too sharp or too blunt, so that the patient cannot bear for the overly sharp spatula to scratch the eye;
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and let your incision, where you peel off that assembly, be slight, so that the membrane returns according to its natural form;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and when all of that assembly is healed, sometimes they use salt water to rinse the eye, and lift it with sweet water, and apply ointment;
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place between the membrane and the eye a pad of linen, and apply to the eye moistened wool soaked in an abundance of egg;
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	And after the third day, use the poultice and moist things until he is well.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the nail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that the nail grows in two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	it is nervous and similar to hard skin, and another that is not nervous, but resembles white frozen moisture, such that when one touches it with iron and thinks to grasp it with forceps, one cannot.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	And both kinds begin near the large tear duct and grow little by little until they cover the entire sight, light, and movement of the eye.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incising is that the patient should place their head on your lap, then proceed with the eyes.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and lift the paper with your hand, then trim the nail at the edges of thin lining, and place it above;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and put on it horsehair, or cowhair, or oxhair, and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the point of the needle slightly and insert it under the nail, then pierce it completely with the needle, and tie the nail with a thread and place it above, and shave off all the hair from the side of the nail that covers the almond and the silk to the tip, then cut the remaining part at the root of the finger as finely as possible with small forces, and leave the natural flesh of the finger so that by the incision no pus comes out habitually;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and sometimes the nail is attached to the bone alone, and by thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then the skin is removed from all the spatium, which is as follows in form:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful that the spatium does not touch the tough membrane and tear it, and that the probe is not punctured;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the incision, sprinkle a little powdered sulfur and some lotion made of litharge into the eye, and leave it until the next day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not attached to a nerve and you cannot insert a needle, and the probe cannot enter, this condition of the nail is often treated with various medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and grow as I have described in the division, and if you wish to cut them, let the patient's eye guide, and take a small, sharp spatula according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And raise the nail gently above, and if you see that it thins slightly and the pus presses against it, then drop from your mouth into the eye a lotion made of litargirium and red collyrium ground fine, and plug the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then proceed with the other work according to this same method until it is completely removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If anything is contrary in the eye, such as a hot abscess, then treat it, and first heal the hot abscess until it is healed, then resume work as before, until it is healthy.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh from the eyelid harms the eye severely, then suspend it at the corner and cut part of it but not all, so that no more tears come from the wound;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then sprinkle on the eye a red collyrium made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that grows over the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	In some people's eyes, red flesh sometimes grows, covering the pupil and restraining over the whites of the eyes, turning them outward, and it looks like a purple flower.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	The procedure is that the patient should place their head on your hand, then you work on the eyes, and carefully remove all that flesh with appropriate hooks, and support it with strength;
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cut the first layer of tissue, and keep cutting with the scraper until the end, and be careful not to injure the eye during the procedure;
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision be made with a spatula as we described for nail cutting and small forceps from which the tissue is removed, as the form after this chapter demonstrates;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the incision is complete and all the flesh is removed, then apply the juice of boiled seeds or pour red collyrium and similar corrosive medicines, and place on top a piece of cotton soaked in egg white, so that it may be secure from a hot abscess.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	And if anything remains and the blood flows out, and you fear a hot abscess, then leave the dressing and treat the hot abscess with things that calm it.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work until it is healed, and thus do when flesh is applied to the eye in this manner.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, it is necessary that you lighten the treatment of each weak eye according to the natural way;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and from the accidental path, in work with iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not place your hand in any of these works until you see that this limb can bear the work.
des voines des eulz	of the veins of the eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Red veins that cover the eye cause discomfort in its function and weaken the eye all day.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	Therefore, first you must check if the eye, in which there is a thorn, is protruding, and there is no other illness except for the thorn;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then treat it in this manner:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to place his head on your lap, then suspend those veins along the entire vein according to your wisdom, and let the veins be delicate twice according to this form:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let two needles be graduated in the body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then when you treat the eye, gently compress those delicate veins, and wipe away the blood hour after hour, until you see the veins recede from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and be careful not to touch the eye with the tips of the spatulas, and perform this work at noon facing the sun, and be very diligent in your work so that you do not miss any veins;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	and when you have done this, apply green and red collyrium to the eye to dissolve what remains of the cataract.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you are unable to collect everything at that hour, apply a poultice to the eye with soothing ingredients for the pain of the eyes, and leave it for several days until the pain is relieved and there is assurance of no hot abscess, then restart according to this method as mentioned before until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	and this is the form of the forces:
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the fistula of the eye
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The physician calls this type of ulcer "arissati":
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	when you treat it with cautery and hot medicines as I have said before, and it does not heal, then there is pus inside that you must incise at the abscess site where it should be opened, and drain all the moisture that is inside until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you see the corruption and blackness, then remove it with all the instruments of which this is the form;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called "aspre chief", and it should be made of fine iron for the head to rotate, and it should be pointed like a file as shown in the present form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the site of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your two fingers, and press your hand a little until you know that the corruption is resolved;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this several times, then restore the site with medicinal extracts.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the flesh is joined and new flesh grows, and the body of the bone is united, and it remains thus for forty days, and it does not renew and is not abscessed, and no bad incident occurs, then you know that it is healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	if not, then there is another condition to bring the fistula to the hole near the navel according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and it is that you uncover the bone a second time with iron, and with medicinal acids, and when it is uncovered take one leaf according to this form, and let the head of the iron be at three angles, and the shaft should be slender until the top as shown here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place it on the bone near the cheekbone, and move your hand away from the eye by one finger's width, then turn completely with the force until it pierces the bone and the patient feels it as the wind enters if he holds his hand over his neck.
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	Then restore the area with dry medicines as I have taught you, and when the flesh grows and hardens the areas, remove the matter from the neck.
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	It is easier for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	From the exit of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eye is fully open and there is no disturbance or reduction in vision, then you must bandage the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then treat it, then apply suction cups without causing injury to draw out fluids, then place on the eye a dressing made of cedar, aloes, incense, and myrrh, and then strain the eye, and cover with bandages and cloths.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And the method of cloths is that you take cloths sufficiently soft, and fold each in four, and then place one upon another according to the quantity that the eyes require;
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then stretch them over a hard bandage formed, and reuse the suction cups to suck without injuring;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the suction cups and leave the eye held tight day and night, and if the ligatures loosen, you must hold them very firmly;
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the ligature after the day and night, and if you see the eye healing, it is good;
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then restart the plasters and the cloths and the bandages and the cupping glasses until he is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	from the rupture of a woven membrane
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When disruption comes in the uvular membrane, it is opened, and pus flows from the paper-like tissue like resin seeds, and it is terrifying to see;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see it necessary to cut, the procedure is such that you insert a needle into the root of the part below up to where it joins above, then insert another needle where there is a double thread from the part near the tear duct;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and you pierce there, and leave the first needle in place according to the position;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cut the area of the double thread and tie a part of the uvula around it tightly, then remove the needle and place on the eye moistened wool soaked in an abundance of egg;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	and leave it until the seed falls with the grape, then treat the eye with comforting remedies until the wound is healed;
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and sometimes the wound is restrained by the grape on all sides with a circle of cloth until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eye shows significant symptoms, pierce it with a fine spatula that comes in perfectly aligned with the eye, and direct the cloudy fluid out and let the eye descend immediately;
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	then extract it until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	from the socket of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease called "alcunnati" is nothing but fluid that has gathered in the eye, resembling water descending, and it is not actually water;
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the manner of the appearance of the work is that you make the patient sit on a prepared and straight seat, then take his head between your hands from both sides, and move it until you see the brow come up to your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then let it be fixed, and do not allow it to descend, and clear the patient's vision so that he can see things as before;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not descend properly, know that it is acute, and if the descent of the brow is not prepared as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	seat the patient between your hands, then take a fine speculum and cut through the transparent membrane along the continuation of the conjunctiva with the transparent membrane and the cornea, until the brow rises;
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when it is issued, drop in the eye hot honey mixed with honey, or hot fenugreek boiled with honey, then treat it further until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	for the waters of the eye
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have described the appearances of the fevers in the division, and what is necessary for puncturing them;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	act according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary for you to seat the patient between your crossed hands, away from the light to avoid sunlight, and hold the healthy eye tightly.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then place the eye patch on your left hand if the eye is left, or on your right hand if the eye is right;
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take in your right hand, if the eye is left, the instrument which is called “almagda”, or with your left hand, if the eye is right;
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument beside the cornea by the thickness of a thread on that white part of the eye near the inner corner, then insert the instrument called “almagda” forcefully, and turn your hand until it penetrates the white part of the eye, and feel when the almagda reaches an empty space;
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	and it is necessary that the length of the path of the almagda be exactly the measure of the space which is from the pupil to the end of the dark part;
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and this is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	you will see the bone through that membrane due to the clarity of the corneal tissue, and then place the instrument up to where the fluid is, then express it gradually one way after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the water flows now, the patient sees before him and the instrument in his eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After resting for a moment, and if the fluid rises again, apply force with the instrument, and when it is firmly placed and no longer rising, then gently extract it by rotating your hand little by little;
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	and then add a bit of honey water to it, and lift the eye out from there.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then place over the eye plugs made of linen soaked in rose oil and an abundance of egg whites, and bind it with a healthy eye.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, apply it mixed with egg whites in abundance.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if alum cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, because there are people who have eyes that are too hard, then you must use the instrument called "alberit," of which this is the form:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	And then pierce only the conjunctiva, and do not go too deep, but act carefully, then insert the instrument as we have said;
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	and at the completion of the work, prepare for the patient a doctor coming, in which he sleeps on his back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	and let him be free of all movements, and give him light foods, and do not move his head neither to the right nor to the left, and bind him according to his condition until the third day;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	then untie him in the same dark house, and test his vision, and show him some things, and then bind him again until the seventh day;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	and it is not appropriate that you do this during the hour of treatment or immediately after incising, but it is necessary to delay this, because the blood rises quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If abscesses come, you should open the eye before the seventh day, and direct it according to one who treats abscesses;
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when it is alleviated, then open the eye and place a small piece of gold over it for some days, and keep it in a dark room immediately.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	And then leave the house gradually, and return to his usual activities.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	And know that no disciple should intervene in this case.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us from Yrach who told us that in his country they make small lancets for drawing off fluid, but nevertheless I have never seen any such thing in our land, nor have I ever read about it in the books of the ancients;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And by chance it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the forms of almonds, so that those who do not recognize them see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they should be made of pure silver:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And let the heads of these be of the same subtlety, and the rear in three acute angles.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh upon the nose
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Sometimes the newly born cartilages appear in various shapes, some of which seem to have many legs like scorpions;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	and there are some in which the cartilage is enlarged with a red hue, and there is underlying healthy cartilage of good color.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In the case of the underlying cartilage that is not enlarged, you should have the patient sit between your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and work his nostrils, and throw the splinter out of those parts, and draw them forth;
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	then proceed as you can sustain the sharp subtle spitum on one side, until you know that the flesh is completely removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains anything that cannot be cut, then scrape it out completely with all the fine instruments gently, so that nothing remains.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if it overflows due to the abscess, then treat it as is appropriate;
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if these are malignant abscesses, then hurry and cauterize until the blood is congealed and all the flesh is removed, then apply to the nose easily and quickly with vinegar or wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If the urine works, and moisture reaches up to the palate, know that he is healthy;
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	and if the moisture does not reach as it should, know that there is flesh on the bone above, where the instrument cannot cut:
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	then you should insert a slightly thick linen thread, and tie it by hand, with each knot spaced appropriately;
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	and place the patient's thread in their nostril as far as possible, and draw it out through smelling until it comes out inside the mouth;
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	and many times children at school do this, and it is an easy thing for one who wants to do it;
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then hold the end that comes from the nape with one hand, and the other end that comes from the mouth with the other hand, and pull them one after the other while observing us who are in the thread.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this until you see that the threads have corrupted the flesh, then pull out the thread, wipe away the blood, and moisten the thread in Egyptian ointment, and put it back in the nose as before;
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the ointment corrupts all that remains of the flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	and then put a piece of lead in the nose for several days until it is healed, and if there is need for drying medicines, use them;
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	and this is the form of the instrument for purging the head, in which one distills oils and medicines through it:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And whether it is made of silver or copper, it resembles an open lamp, like a chain, and the conduit is similar.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you prefer, make a closed chain, and let the instruments be full for purging the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and it should have a handle at the top to hold when heating the oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	of the flesh upon the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times a disease called "telul" arises on the head of the nose, and it grows until it becomes large, appearing as a visible object when looking at it;
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And for this reason it is necessary that you cut it at the beginning, and remove all hair, then place upon it the cautery or burning medicine;
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	and if you delay cutting it until it is large, be wary if it is hard, of dark color, and if the patient has poor sensation:
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	do not touch it with iron because it is an embedded abscess, for when you cut it even once, it brings great harm to the patient;
