de la routure de l’artere	Of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is cut, and the skin above it is sealed, abscesses often occur, and the same happens with a swollen vein and an abscess;
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and one knows it thus when it is due to the artery, as the abscesses are long and deep;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	and when you feel it with your fingers, you sense the tightness;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	and when it is due to the vein, it appears swollen and protruding;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	and it is foolish to incise this abscess, especially when it is near the armpits and elbows and on the neck and in many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	It is therefore necessary to avoid treatment with iron, and one who has a head injury should also be avoided, and in the case of arterial swelling on the long bone, make an incision above the skin;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	then work the area with bandages, and carefully separate the artery from the tissues until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	then insert a needle from one side and pierce it to the other side, and tie off the artery with a double thread in two places, as I have taught you for the extraction of the two arteries found in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	then puncture the area between the two ligatures with an instrument so that the blood flows out which is inside, and release the abscess;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	then apply the treatment for bowel movement, until the stool is liquid;
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat them with appropriate ointment until they are healed;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	and if the abscess is near a vein, you must mark with your hand as much of the abscess as you can on the skin, then insert the needle beneath the area marked by your hand, and pierce it, using double thread so that you draw it out from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	then tie the abscess, as I have told you, with one end of the thread to each of the two threads;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	and if you fear that the thread might come loose, insert another needle along the entire length of the thread under the abscess from the incision of the first needle, and tie the threads in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut open the abscess until the excess matter comes out, then cut away the excess from the heart and leave those that are tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply a moist bandage soaked in wine and oil, then treat with patches and ointments until he is well.
des apostemes des ners	abscesses of the nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Just as abscesses occur in the artery and vein, abscesses also occur in the nerves when they are injured, or from excessive labor, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this happens more often in the shoulders and elbows and in all places where there are joints, and these are severe abscesses, and their color resembles the skin color, and they cause significant pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	and when it is pressed firmly, the patient feels pain, and it is not throughout the body but rather near the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	and it is fixed in all directions, and does not go forward or backward, nor up or down, and those that are in joints should not be cut with a knife:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	by chance there might be a contraction;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	and for those who have it at the head or forehead, cut the skin with a scalpel.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, grasp it with forceps and cut it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if it is large, suspend it with an ounce, and scrape it, then remove it and stitch the wound together, and treat it until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	large hanging mouths
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	At times, this occurs in bellies and not elsewhere, a disease called "fungus" due to its appearance, with subtle roots and large lumps;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are both small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	and I saw a man who had two on his stomach which looked more like mushrooms than anything else, and there was no difference between them, they were white, and they had fine roots, and moisture corroded them quickly.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them out and found one weighed eighteen ounces and the other six, and in performing this work during the incision you must observe if the patient is moist, and the color of the flesh is white and moist with a fine root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	cut it with a broad spatula, and have the fire cautery ready at hand.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For in cutting there often come excessive flows of blood, and if the blood overcomes you, then hasten to use the cautery;
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient afraid and fearful of the incision with iron, then take a well-made silk thread, and tie the artery as we have said, and leave it for two days;
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	and then restrain it, and do not stop compressing the silk thread until it cuts through the artery, and cease from further work;
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are thick, be wary of cutting them directly for fear of the abdomen, but you may safely cut half of it, then use the cautery so that it does not regrow;
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	Then treat the wound, and take care not to cut the tendon which is of purple color and little sense and milk-white appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an embedded abscess, and I will come to the treatment of ulcers shortly thereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	when the wound becomes hot
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of swelling comes from a cautery on a wound or tear on the surface, and it is on the abdomen and some of the bowels are involved, as happens in other ruptures, or from blood that flows from veins or arteries according to what precedes, or from windiness;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	and if this is due to the rupture of the surface and the exit of the bowel, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the skin, it causes little pain, and is clear from various openings.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if this is due to the issue from the intestine, then it becomes more diverse, and when one presses on both sides, it swells up, and then returns, and perhaps it is congested, and greatly enlarges at the entrance of the bath and for hard work.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if this is due to moisture, it is a minor issue, and clearly apparent when you press it with your hand, it does not constrain.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if it is due to blood, these signs clearly indicate large and hard abscesses, and they are set according to a certain quantity;
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is due to windiness, it is shallow to probe, and the procedure is that you observe whether the appearance is due to arterial blood, or from a vein, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	It is necessary that you leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For there is doubt and fear about it, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if the appearance is due to the intestine or the eye, then you must instruct the patient to hold their breath, and lie completely straight, then incise all around the edge;
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	then instruct them to lie quietly in your hands, then go around the place where you have marked with all the spatula, then extend half of the abscess above with the large forceps;
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then bind the area tightly with a strong thread or a rope of strong silk, and let the bandage be firmly applied.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then work on half of the abscess extended over the bandage, and place your index finger there, and seek the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	if you find it caught in the bandage, then undo it, and push the intestine back into the abdomen.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	and if you find the bowel, grasp it with your finger, and cut away the excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	and if the artery or vein opposes you, go around them gently, then return to your work and take two needles, and insert two threads outside, and place the two needles around what you have done in a cross shape to pierce.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then incise the abscess in four places over the needles, and if you wish, remove the needles, and leave the wound until it matures, and the dead tissue will come out by itself;
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	when you cut it when it is subtle and ripe, then treat it as necessary, and drain the abscess as we have said;
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	and draw out the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the wound as necessary, and close the wound.
dou chancre	of the ulcer/gangrene
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have discussed in the section the similarities of ulcers, and how one should treat them with medications, and how to avoid treatment with iron;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	and we say that an ulcer in the armpit is dangerous, and great caution is needed in its treatment, and the ancients said that when ulcers are in places where they can be scraped out like those on the breast, and on the thigh, and in similar areas, they should be completely removed at the beginning;
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	And when it is large and old, you must not approach it, for I have never seen anyone heal it.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	nor has anyone ever healed it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And when the work is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, you should occasionally purge the patient of black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then make the patient healthy if there is obvious fullness, then position the patient properly to perform the work;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then apply your ointments to the ulcer, and clean it thoroughly from all parts, leaving nothing behind;
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	Let the blood flow freely, and press firmly with your hand or some object on the area, and if the bleeding from the wound opposes incising the artery or vein, then cauterize until the blood is staunched;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it further until it is healed.
de ydropisie	Of hydropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have already mentioned in the division the similarities of dropsy, and how the gathering of fluid is formed, and the signs of each similarity, and the treatment which is done with medicine, and that which is treated by iron:
si est eclites soulement;	it is solely edema;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	and one should not use iron in these two similarities:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	That is to say, tympanitis and ileus, for these are deadly things;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when you treat this appearance of dropsy which is called "eclipsis" with medicines, and the treatment does not help, then look to see if the patient is weak, or if he has another illness besides dropsy, such as coughing and releasing of bowels and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	do not use iron, for there is doubt;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	and if you see the patient is very strong, and he has no other illness than dropsy alone, and he is neither too young nor too old, then you should proceed as follows:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	lift the patient up on your hands, and have an assistant press the abdomen by pushing the liquid to the lowest part of the belly, then take the spatula according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And let there be cutting from two sides.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	Use a sharp point, and ensure it is not so deep that it can reach the intestine when inserted, and it cannot be withdrawn;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	then check if the edema has spread towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	if necessary, you should cut three fingers above the navel directly over the groin;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the edema is due to liver disease, your incision should be three fingers to the left of the navel;
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to the spleen, it should be on the right, and the patient must not lie on the incision so that the excess fluids do not flow to the weaker area;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	Then pierce the entire skin with the instrument, and cut it open, and lift your hand to all the fat between the skin and muscle as when flaying to the quantity of a nail or around.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Then cut into the muscle until the fat comes to the place of eight, and this is where the fluid is, then draw it out, and insert this instrument which has the shape:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it resembles a fine silver chain, and is made of reed or light rush, and has at the middle a small hole;
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side, three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one elsewhere;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is cut like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that the writer makes on the feather:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at the top above is the blade, so that when the instrument comes to the tip, it now descends upon the instrument;
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty then half or one third of it, for if you empty more than is necessary at that hour, by chance the patient may die from the spirit's reaction to the weapon, or they fall fainting, or approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty according to the quantity of its strength, and according to what the signs of the patient's disposition indicate, and their pulse;
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	Then draw the instrument and retain the fluid, and it is now retained by the heart which plugs the aperture that is above the diaphragm, of which I have spoken, that you pierce according to this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	Then restart the instrument on the following day if you see that the patient is suffering from it, and draw out a small amount of fluid;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	Do this for several days, and be careful not to overdo it so that only a little bit of fluid remains.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	And if you are uncertain about the patient and leave a lot of fluid in them, then treat them with burial herbs or hot sand, and by sweating a lot or bathing in the sun, and let them drink lots of fluids;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And treat with drying medications until he is healthy, and cauterize on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of the fluid, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	about the numbness of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born who have no opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary to pierce it immediately with a very fine spatula according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	then place a fine cloth plug in the opening, and secure it for three or four days, and when he wishes to urinate, remove the plug, allow him to urinate, and then replace it;
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	and sometimes this is not necessary, because the urine that comes from force does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	He whose opening is small should be treated with the cloth of flax as we have said, and it will enlarge.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the opening in its place are defective, for some are born with the opening at the head of the penis, so they cannot urinate unless they lift their penis upwards;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	and they cannot heal because the matter cannot reach the bone marrow, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method of the procedure is that the patient lies supine on their back, then holds the rod and places it as thick as a quill's middle part, so that the hole in the head fits exactly, as is appropriate;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be careful of bleeding that often occurs, and if it happens, stop the bleeding as one would stop blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	pimples on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	Often these ulcers come in the rod, and it is an ugly appearance of flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	And there are malignant and non-malignant ones;
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	You should grasp them with a fine needle, cut and clean all of them, then apply cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment;
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with diafinicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, of putrid color and foul-smelling, then you must apply a cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the dart is in the shaft of the penis, and part is inside the skin and part outside, then you must remove the part that is inside first;
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	and when it is sealed, then treat what is outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat it all at once, the head of the penis is not secure and may be pierced, leading to blackening and corruption in the shaft of the penis and the testicles;
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	It is necessary to remove everything that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster made of pomegranate peel and vinegar, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, then treat with a lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	The cauterization helps with both conditions simultaneously:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	that is to say, for the hemorrhage and for the corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	and if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, then it is necessary to insert a tube of lead into its canal, and have the patient urinate through it;
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	and when the hair is irritated at the head of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, whether it results in a wound or an abscess, then you must burn it with a pointed instrument until the tissue is loosened, and free the head of the penis from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	And if this is difficult to discuss, then you must scorch it with some poultice at the top of the shaft and of the blade;
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	Then carefully separate them between two, and place a fine linen cloth moistened in cold water between them so that they do not adhere again.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	Circumcision is not a dislocation of continuity like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Still, when we perform this act of our own will, and especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best work, and the least harmful for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not speak of circumcision for their children, because they did not practice it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the majority of masters and senior practitioners who performed circumcisions around the dawn, and with great force, and all at once.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	So bind them tightly because there are two cloths, and by chance one may cut the upper one and leave the lower one untouched.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now there is danger in cutting it again, and the pain doubles, and the healing of the bone is not assured.
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	and in the healing of the nail, by chance the iron may slip, and ruin the work, and often they heal without needing treatment as I have observed.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleansing that is done with force to the entire limb of thread I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the force cuts precisely both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand, cut evenly in one single motion;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	but make sure the thread is tight around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	And the method of the first procedure is that you make the child, if he understands, think that you are only tying a thread around the shaft, and then you can delight him in all ways that you can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	Then hold him straight between your hands, and place the forceps between your hands or behind your feet where the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then place your hand on the shaft and blow at the root, and pull it up until the head of the shaft is in place;
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Then clean it well of the debris that has accumulated there, then tie the site with a doubled thread, then tie from one pouch to another.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	and hold at the two dobs by the second ligature on the pouched part and thumb, then lift the heart quickly and draw the head of the rod.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then allow the blood to flow drop by drop, for this is safer;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and apply powder and then on top of the powder place a piece of cloth glued with one yolk of an egg diluted with rose water, cooked well and fresh, and leave it there until the next day, and treat it again as needed until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of force for purification is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two edges should be sharp and the edges should be as wide as the blade evenly:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the mistake in cleansing is when the pus inside goes to the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	then it is necessary that you extend it to your nail, just as the doctors treat an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it to your nail, then hold it with forceps, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they exceed three days, and the area below the thigh is swollen, wait until the abscess has subsided somewhat, and then gently scrape it;
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	cut it as much as you can without harming the area of the thigh, for it will do no harm to that part.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Treat then the wound with powder, which we have mentioned in the chapter on powders, and if one cuts into the heart beyond measure, and it goes too far, it will do no harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat it then as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is due to the obstruction of a stone, or coagulated blood, or a tumor, or dead tissue, or similar things, which we have mentioned in the section;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	and if the urine is not released and you see that the retention is due to a stone that is lodged in the neck of the bladder, then it is necessary for the patient to be seated on their knees;
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	and place the feet on the back, extend his belly from above the back, and restrain the patient's thigh as much as he can;
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	and then the neck of the bladder is pressed to expel the stone upwards, so that the urine is released;
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction with all the instruments called "syringe," of which here is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it should be made of thin silver, as fine as the feather of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and let the tube be one and a half palms long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the manner of the urine flow is that you take a double thread, and tie at the top a piece of wool or cotton, and put the end of the thread into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and trim the excess of the wool and push it up to the top of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair, and lubricate the bladder and penis with moistened oil and olive oil and cold water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the base of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the body;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and feel when the patient senses that the container is empty, but this should not be done if the path it follows is twisted;
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch the wool thoroughly bit by bit, and the urine follows the wool, then extract it forcefully, and let the urine flow.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and repeat the suction until the bladder is empty, and let the patient be comfortable.
des maladies de la vessie	diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When pus or blood comes to the bladder, and putrefaction is assembled there, and you wish to introduce liquids and medicines, use all the instruments which are called "clepsydre," and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the leather covering through which the medication tube is such that it stops up the penis well without addition, so one can draw out moisture and insert when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you wish to administer your medicines into the bladder, place the head of the syringe in the moisture, and draw it out with the extractor that is inside;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	So you will draw the moisture to the site, and then firmly set it by pulling it in;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	The moisture will enter in and reach the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the form of the subtle enema with which one enemas the bladder:
si est ci:	this is as follows:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	It is of silver or rush, and the head is higher;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	and displace it to the side where the ligament falls;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture with which you wish to enema the bladder in it, then tie it between the two breasts tightly with a good strong string, and heat the container of that moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then insert the head of the enema into the penis, then pull your hand along the bladder to push all the liquid upwards until the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make a circle, piercing it roundly;
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	then insert a strong thread into these holes, then attach the circle as you would a sieve, and place inside it what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument;
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already stated in the division the manners of stones and their extraction together with medicines;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	and I have stated the difference between the stone formed in the kidneys, and all the signs, and which stones one should work to cut;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	and in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is formed in the bladder happens more often to children, and this is a sign that the urine jumps from the bladder similar to how it does in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and there is clear pain, and the patient scratches his penis, and he does this many times, and then it constricts;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and in many cases the foundations are weakened;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing of children is easy until they are four years old, and it is very difficult in the elderly, and it is moderate for those who are between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	and the treatment is easier for those who have large stones than for those who have small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to purify the patient with an enema, to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes obstructs in seeking to remove the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift them up and move them backward so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and it sometimes comes out from a higher place;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have the patient sit between your hands which are prepared behind their thighs so that the bladder is completely tilted downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then press and touch inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in the space, then hurry now to cut into the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall out upon touching with your thumb, moisten your index finger with oil from your left hand, if the patient is female, or your middle finger, if the patient is an adult male;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and insert it into its place, and feel for the stone, and when you sense it with your finger, gently push it towards the bladder neck;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press with your finger, and push it out where you intend to make the incision.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and tell him to stretch out his right hand towards the groin, and with his left hand remove the skin that is underneath the groin in the area where the waist is made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then place the spatula cutting it, which is its shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between the groin and the anus, not in the middle but towards the left side of the navel;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and it should be straight over the stone, and your two hands should immediately be at the anus, and the incision should traverse the area so that it is wide on top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	by chance the pressure is so strong at the base that it leaps forward without effort;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and you know there are some stones with corners and edges:
si est griés a issir;	it is difficult to remove;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and there are some that are smooth, like a hawk's talon, and round, from which removal is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	For those with corners and edges, make the tool larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if it does not leap forward, then you must clamp with pliers that are like a file at the top, to firmly grip the stone so it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	where you place beneath the eye a curved delicate instrument;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot do it thus, enlarge the socket and the aperture, and if blood escapes, then constrict it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there are more than one stone, place the larger one at the neck of the bladder first, then cut above it, and pull it out forcefully, and do the same for the smaller ones if there are any.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, you must observe it and make a larger incision.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	either he dies, or the urine comes out immediately so that the wound cannot close;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but still, strive to extract it, or use pincers to break it apart, until you remove it piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And when you have completed your work, apply the wound with incense and aloes and dragon's blood, and compress it, and place over it a damp cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then lay the patient on their back, and do not loosen the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you release it, wash the area thoroughly with oil and water, then treat it with diafinicon ointment and basilicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses and corrosion come to the wound, and clots of blood in the bladder, and thus the urine is retained, which occurs in such a manner that it must be expelled with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	insert your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will rot the bladder.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then lift the wound of water and ease and healing, and assist it in all ways that you know, until it is healed;
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that every time you treat it, you bind the two thighs together, and apply the medicines to the place.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small and it is in the passage of the penis, lodged inside, and the urine cannot exit;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	then treat it as I say thus, that you cut it many times, for this treatment excuses the cutting.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already tested this in this way.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	Take an iron fork according to this form and have three prongs fixed in one handle:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take some thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot move backward into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then insert the probe gently into the shaft until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	and turn the probe gently in your hand within the stone bit by bit until you can pierce the stone from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	the urine will soon come, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the shaft.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	It will be broken immediately, and the stone will pass with the urine, and the patient will be cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, tie a thread below the stone and another above it, then cut the shaft directly through the stone between the two ties, then extract the stone, and untie the ligatures, and clean the congealed blood in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until he is healthy.
de la piere des femmes	of women's stones (referring to kidney stones or similar conditions)
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	It rarely happens that a stone is formed in women, and when it does occur once, the treatment is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	one reason is that the woman may be a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	and the second reason is that one cannot find a woman who knows and will expose herself to doctors, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third reason is that by chance one cannot find a woman who knows this art of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	and the fourth reason is that the stone in a woman is harder by nature than the stone in a man, so it requires a deeper cut, and there is great fear involved. And if necessity arises for this, you must take a wise midwife who knows well, and finding one is difficult, and if you do not find one, pray to God with all your might.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present a wise woman in the lives of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command regarding the investigation of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look very carefully if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then she must insert her finger into the fundament and search for the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, she should press the stone out with her finger, and recommend that she inserts her finger into the patient's vagina and presses firmly with her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she must gently move the stone from the entrance of the bladder down to below, until it reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut above the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the anus, where it is moved, and feel for the stone in that part;
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move his hand above the stone or below it, and let the waist be slightly bent;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the instrument into the waist, if you feel the stone then enlarge the wound so that the stone can come out, and know that there are many kinds of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	that is to say, small and large and rough and smooth, long and round, and those that have spines.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	and know the signs to understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if the blood flows, then place vitriol powder at the site, and keep it there for an hour until the bleeding stops;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work until the stone is expelled, and have the instruments that I told you about for extracting stones from people to help in your work;
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	and if the blood flows and it comes from the artery that is severed, put the powder on the site and bind with cloths and linen, and do not attempt to extract again, and leave the stone unextracted, for the patient might die;
puis cure la plaie.	then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is appeased, and the swelling subsides, then return to your work, until the stone is expelled.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Aquous humor is nothing other than a collection of moisture or white substance, which comes from the testicles, contained in the egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	and it is called "white substance," and sometimes it is properly within the membrane of the egg, so one might think it is another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and this is the skin of the penis between the white shaft that we have mentioned;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	and this does not occur unless it is diseased.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this aqueous retention is due to weakness that affects the testicles, and this matter spreads out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from striking the genitals, and this moisture can have many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	it may be a color inclining to yellow, or without redness, or black, or watery white, and this happens more frequently;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this condition, for if it is on the white shaft that we have mentioned, then the abscesses are frequent, the swelling long like the shape of an egg, and does not reveal the genitals, because there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the proper tissue, then the abscesses are soft with part of the egg, and because of this, people think it is another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the eyes and the white membrane, then one can feel it well;
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	then when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all around the affected area, as its form was described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what follows after the introduction, judge what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron, the patient must be bled according to his strength and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then lay him on his back on something slightly raised, and place many cloths under him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and instruct the attendant to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs below the heart.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the spatula and cut the skin of the genitals in a straight line from top to bottom until near the base, and make your incision entirely straight while carefully cutting through the skin down to the white tissue, and peel it off delicately as much as possible.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then puncture the area full of fluid with a wide incision, and drain out all the fluid, and then apply your forceps, and stretch the tissue upward.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the heart of the genitals, but only the skin.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cut through it all or piece by piece carefully for him subtly, that if you do not cut it well wisely, the fluid will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	and if the eye jumps during your work, then reset it in its place when you have completed the work of the operation.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then sew the two leaves of the groin together at one seam, then treat it as other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the eye corrupted by another disease, then it is necessary to tie the vessels that are suspensory, fearing the loss of blood;
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the groin at all the suspensory parts, and extract the eye, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if heat is assembled in two parts together, know that these are two roots;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	if you cut the other part just as you did the first equally, then wipe away the blood, and put linen soaked in rose oil on the wound;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and place another layer of linen soaked in wine and oil over it, and put two cloths on top, and cover with doubled cloth, and tie it securely according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two cloths, and wrap them with linen strips according to this appearance and sew them together at the waist of the pants, one going from the buttocks up to the back, and the other to the side part;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two heads on each of the two rings, and let all the straps be fastened in the buckle of the bracer;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and sometimes this area is treated with a cautery instead of an iron incision, and you should take a fine knife-shaped cautery, cut the skin over the testicles, and heat it as we have said, so that the white substance containing the fluid is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	take the cautery in this shape, and pierce that white substance with tongs, and scrape it with this fine hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And cut in all the ways that you can, until you scrape it all clean;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and guard that the fire does not touch the eye;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and know that this work is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and use caution to prevent loss of blood, and be careful with the procedures of cutting;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything goes contrary, such as an abscess or loss of blood or another thing, then treat what is contrary according to what was said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to wait for this procedure due to its horror, then administer perforation as I tell you, and when you are certain by the signs we have mentioned that aqueous fluid is there, have the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	Then pierce the abscess on the side completely along the entire span of the body, and make the incision along the length of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and let the opening be wide so that all the fluid can run out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then place cotton on the area, and secure it, and leave it so that the remaining fluid can drain, then treat the wound until it is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow the fluid to exit from the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a quill or instrument used for treating the fluid in hydropics, as described above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and enlarge the pit of the wound, and note that the fluid returns after about six months or thereabouts, and when it has gathered as before, thus the patient will live out their days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that during the cutting of this vein there is fear in many cases, for which reason it seems better to let it be.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses occur in the body, especially in the groin;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and this is due to many causes.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is known to be due to sour and sharp excess, which spreads in the groin, or from impact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess is according to the color of the skin;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and does not feel any pain, and there is a severe abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and by chance, some severe abscesses are fearful and stone-like, and of a bad color, and sometimes they come from the artery or swelling of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from the artery, it is known by the hot disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it is not appropriate for you to touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	Those who have swelling from a vein are known by their condition through the expression of feeling when touched with fingers, and one can properly diagnose this and other conditions based on this.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And it is that you cut the groin artery, then place the egg above, and draw it out from the white membrane, and release the suspensory of all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hardened with these new veins, then you must draw out the egg, and cut it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is air in the membrane, or within what is inside the vessels, then you must release all that cavity, and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is at the back, then you must cut it all away, and extract the eye, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is complete, apply the wound with wet wool in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapping similar to bark, with the softening of the groin, and the patient moves very painfully when he goes.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment for this disease is as well very fearful as the one before, and nevertheless we shall tell you about it, according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	It is necessary that you make the patient sit on a raised chair, then place the suspensory below the testicles up to your two hands, and hold firmly the parts near the penis, and stretch them strongly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	then cut open the scrotum with a broad sharp spatula across the parts, until they are exposed, and then scrape from each side, as we have said in the extraction of arteries that are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then insert a needle with doubled thread and tie it at the first place where the vein is, and tie it again to the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them directly in the middle, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted humors;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as you would others where you insert a boule, so that no vessel bleeds that nourishes one of the testicles;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for by this no harm comes, and if it happens to all the vessels, then it is necessary to draw out the testicles from all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the testicle does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the fracture of the cheekbone
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The occurrence of this condition is due to the section that comes from the syphilis, or the extension on the abdomen in the groin area, because the intestines descend through that opening to one of the testicles;
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this rupture is in the thigh or from extending it, and these two manners come from many causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	by striking, jumping, lifting heavy loads, or similar actions;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is from extending the thigh are that they occur little by little over a long time, and do not happen suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are equal up to the bottom, because the thigh is close to the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs when it is from the section of the cheekbone are that they cause a sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear differently, near the skin, because of the exit of the intestine and the body pulling away from the cheekbone.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the intestines descend with the bowel, and it is retained inside, causing great pain for the patient, especially when it is compressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments there is fear, for which one should avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to insert his finger into the wound inside the intestines if it can be reached;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then bind around his neck. between your hands, and lift the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then stretch the heart above it, and cut away all the skin from the genitals gently;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then insert hooks into the sides of the waist according to what you need to open the wound, and make them such that the eye can pass through;
