puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then peel off the skin that is above the skin of the genitals, until the white fatty tissue is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then insert your index finger in the area behind the genitalia, between the white fatty tissue that is below the skin of the penis and the second layer of fat, and separate what is behind the penis and between the second layer of fat;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	And then move with the right hand inside the groin area, and stretch the white skin upwards with your left hand, and lift the egg across the entire surface towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	And instruct the assistant to stretch the egg upwards and undo those who are tied behind;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	And ask your two assistants if there is any part of the intestines wrapped around the white skin, and if you find anything, push it back into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	Then take a needle with a thick thread made of several strands and insert it into the back part of the skin, which is behind the groin area;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	After the waist, then cut the threads that appear to be strands until there are four strands;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	Then he assembles them one on top of the other in the manner of a cross, and binds the surface, which we have mentioned is beneath the skin of the genitals, with a strong thread from two sides;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	Then wrap the head with threads and bind it firmly from two sides so that none of the vessels that nourish it can enter inside, preventing an abscess from forming;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the thread again according to the first binding for two digits long, and after these two bindings leave the surface that is beneath the skin of the genitals exposed for one digit;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then bind everything else according to the roundness that the egg carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	Then cut in the part which is away from the skin of the scrotum, until the blood flows, and the bowel, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	Then apply moistened wool in oil to the wounds, and bind it as we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the pale surface we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, due to fear of blood loss.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens often, and leave the bandage on until it falls off by itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays in falling off, soak it in hot water and place what we have said on it until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another method until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to treat it with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is made like the vine tendrils that wrap around the branch, in such a way that you tie the vessels, above the waist lightly at the back;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut it open, and treat the abscess of the one who works, until the pus flows;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes there is a rupture in the groin, as we have said, and the place becomes apparent;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and no internal organs descend to the thighs, and if they do descend, it is serious, and must be repaired at all times;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and if it remains in this condition for too long, the wound or tissue will become inflamed, until the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens due to the stretching of the tissue in the groin area, as we have said, because it is stretched, then becomes softened and swollen and visible;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	And the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And sometimes it is treated with an iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	And the patient lies supine on their back between your hands, then cover the swollen area of the fracture with a pad about three fingers wide;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	And then remove the padding that is under the skin as follows, then take the thread and place it on the visible area of the pad;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press it firmly to the abdomen, then stitch the two visible areas of the pad at the head of the thread, and sew one and the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then extract the head of the shaft, and do not cut into the surface or extend the egg or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of the root of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Then treat it according to the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, heal and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The suture is tight, and there is no appearance of it in the rupture, and the cauterizations are soft in this place, and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the testicles becomes soft in some men, because the tissues inside are softened, and it appears milky.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	and when one wishes to treat it, have the patient lie on his back, and cut the soft skin over the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	then sew the two lips together with one seam, and if you wish, stitch the excess soft skin to three or four places firmly;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then cut between the seams, and treat it as other wounds, until it is healed, and sew it up.
dou chastrement	of the punishment
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that castration is condemned in our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to speak of it in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is not necessary except for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one of which is that the priest knows how to answer when asked, and knows the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say then that castration is performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	By attraction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the one we do by attraction, make the animal sit in hot water until the joint is softened and hanging.
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them in your hand until they are reset and you no longer feel any discomfort.
Du chastrement de taille:	On castrating the flanks:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	you should hold the animal still, and press the skin around the flanks with your left hand, then tie the suspensory bandage, and cut each side separately when you have properly skinned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave some of the fatty tissue and the thin layer of fat that is on the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	And this method of castration is more severe than that which is done by traction, because with traction some part of the testicles might remain, causing the animal to desire lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism exists in two forms among men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one in which between the two testicles there is an opening as the figure of a woman's body, where there may be hair, and sometimes it encircles the urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is for women, and place on the finger as thick as a rod and two eggs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for both man and woman is that you cut away all adjacent tissues, and treat them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for those whose urine sprays on the skin of the genitals, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of tension or strain
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigene is a condition fitted onto the natural part, so that it appears too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	and some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the condition.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary to paint the excess of the tentigene on your hand or fingernails, and then cover it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not go too deep, so that no blood comes out, then treat the condition with another treatment until it is healed;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and for another condition that appears at the entrance of the mouth and spreads, and occasionally becomes worse, it resembles a cow's tongue, and therefore the ancients called it "cow sickness.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	It is necessary that you treat it as we have said about tendinitis, and care for it until it is healed.
de erratique	Of erratic/erratic nature
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic is it when the nature of a woman is not perceived, or the passage is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or accidental due to illness that has come there;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or it is due to added flesh, or from a thick or thin membrane, and it is formed perfectly in the abdomen, or on the sides, or within, or wherever;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and prevents conception and childbirth, and perhaps the onset of menstruation;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the knowledge of these things is by examining the opening.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If constipation is closely apparent, then use either of my two methods or the right one.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is from a thin membrane and it is close to the two leaves, then hurry, and treat thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Place your two hands together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then press the two thighs firmly together until the finer parts are flat, and place them over the abdomen;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take linen, and soak it in oil, and place it on the area, and have the woman lie on her back each day so that it does not dry.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the sore is hard and thick, then you should cut it with a scalpel resembling a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the swelling is from flesh growth, suspend it to the onceine and the hip;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the blood-stanching medicines ready, such as hawthorn, dragon's blood, incense, mixed with an abundance of egg;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then apply a piece of leather wide enough so that the wound cannot close.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and let it be for a long time, and then dress the wound with a dry linen bandage;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	and continue treating it until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when flesh becomes corrupted in a wound, it must be cut according to this manner, except for deeply seated abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For in the deeply seated abscess that is in the wound, one should not attempt to cut it open.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that occur without proper treatment, and when hemorrhoids become old they harden.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have already mentioned in the section the appearances of them, and the signs, and I will say here those that respond to treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that when hemorrhoids and hard growths are thoroughly embedded in the wound and do not respond to sensation, they cannot be cured by cautery.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who have a sore on their mouth, which can be felt, are those who can be treated by cleaning.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	Therefore, you must place the woman in a cold room, then extract the hemorrhoid with forceps, and cut it off at its roots, then apply powder made from substances that constrict blood flow, such as oak bark and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then place his feet against the wall for an hour, then put them in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if bleeding occurs, have him sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate rind and gall and similar things, and then take barley flour, mix it with honey and oil, and make a plaster for his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops flowing, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, apply cupping to the back and breasts without injuring them;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take wool, and moisten it in plantain juice or in elderberry juice with old wine, and apply to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has subsided, treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And the one called "albathir" is red, and it resembles a rough head, so it must be cut as I have said about the thul.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	For abscesses of the flesh
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses occur in the flesh, such as cankers and stone abscesses and herpes and ulcers and fistulas and hemorrhoids and hot abscesses, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	Therefore, I must speak in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes in the buttocks, which is not one of those that occur in the bowel.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	And if you wish to know the treatment with iron, observe whether the abscess is sharp at the beginning of its appearance, and full of heat and fever, and if it turns red when you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it come to a head until the pain is alleviated;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	Then make the patient sit on one chair, and have two small chairs where he can lean, and support his back and bring his legs together away from the injured leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	And let his thighs be spread apart, and place his arms under his knees, and bind them tightly with a good cloth;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	Then give him the tool toward the right side, and bring the instrument used to work the mouth of the dislocation, which will be described in detail afterward;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	And it is necessary that when you bring this instrument to him, you insert the tip first to determine the depth of the dislocation so that what enters does not go too deep and does not harm the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not cause pain;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and he should place the tip of the instrument above, and hold the instrument firmly.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess is ready to be opened, and it is cut by hand gently, then it should be cut at the top, in the spongy area.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the abscess is emptied, you should place moistened lint in rose oil, or in green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and place the lint inside the wound at its base, and cover it with clean, moistened wool soaked in water or decoction of mallows outside the wound.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat after two days of applying ointment as needed, until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes lift the woman and cleanse the wound with a mixture of water and honey, and then use water or a decoction of lily roots and agrimony.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	Then return to applying ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is covered with a poultice, then you should avoid treating it with iron, but treat it as we have said in the section.
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the signs of natural childbirth, and these are evident when you see the woman strain downwards, and desire to smell the air:
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child hastens to come out.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that this childbirth is according to the natural form, and the passage is under his head, and the afterbirth follows with it;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his belly so that the child comes out quickly;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	for when it descends upon its head, the placenta comes with it, and the woman is cleansed of her excesses through proper purification;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and those who come in another way do not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes upon its feet, and emerges from the thighs or hands, or appears on its belly or backside, and turns by chance onto its neck, or in other bad positions;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and subtle in these matters, and to guard against error and deception, and I will show you all the positions how one should assist her.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child comes out head first by natural means, and the woman gives birth heavily, and the strength of the mother is weak, then let her sit on a chair, or where women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and prepare her nature with oil or fenugreek that has been cooked, and then place a basin between her two thighs, as described in the form of a small spatula:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and split the membrane, and cut until the moisture inside comes out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press the woman's abdomen until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then it is necessary to give her an enema of fenugreek muscilago with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her sniffle and sneeze with conditi, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Now remove the foreign object.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands dislocate, you must reset them gently bit by bit;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot enter, place the woman on a chair and lift her feet up;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then raise the chair off the ground, and support the woman so she does not fall when standing;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hand cannot enter and the foreign object is dead, cut the hand with the knife that is placed here beforehand, and remove the object, then reset it gently.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of delivering the child onto her feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child stands on its feet, one must elevate it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take one foot and stretch it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps up to the thighs, instruct them to grasp it, and make it sneeze from condition;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	and may it jump free if God wills it.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not go as we have said, turn it little by little until it is in its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it moves easily.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come free as we have instructed, take mastic from the tree, sesame oil, and melted gum, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and place the woman's nature within and remove her from this ointment, then have her sit in warm water up to below the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened below, apply the myrrh collar to her and place it underneath, then let her stay for one hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on the chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and gently press her abdomen, for the child is now jumping.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the issue of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this form, let the bailie place his hands little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let her be lifted by her neck, and hang her feet down, and lie her on the bed;
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bend his hands little by little, and then take his hands on the belly, and remove the cushions below, until she is prepared to go down;
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if the child does not jump, take his feet and move them forward, then push up his belly, then put your hands underneath;
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and bring the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and instruct the woman to hold on as long as the child descends.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the issue of the child that comes with one hand hanging out
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	It is necessary for the surgeon to return the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if it cannot be returned, help the woman stand and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, make her lie on the bed, and straighten her legs fully;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then manipulate the muscle as I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, make her sit on the chair, then study how to return the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and hold the child according to its natural position, and make her sneeze, and instruct her to pull as soon as the baby starts coming out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the birth of the child on its neck, and have her spread out her hands, and her face turned towards her mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is necessary that the bailiff hold his hand, then turn it little by little, and hold it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, apply the natural manipulation with salt and oil as we have said, then instruct her to move little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	and when you have done this, make her sit on a chair, and instruct her to grasp it;
et la fai esternuer.	and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	In the same manner for the entire second part
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes to the second swelling in this manner, cut the swelling to your nail, until the moisture is emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the swelling appears on their face and neck, cut it from the mouth so that it is not obstructed, and relieve the swelling;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then insert the child as needed, and instruct the woman to grasp something several times:
adonques si istra legierement.	then gently extract it.
de l’issue des gemelz	about the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that jaundice often occurs, and sometimes three or four times;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not a strange thing, it often happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	These are strange things, and they do not live unless rarely.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they multiply and are separated by the surface which divides them, which is attached to the bud;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they emerge as naturally as any others, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they emerge forcefully, treat them as we have said, and let the surgeon be skilled, and do quickly and gently what he does.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do as he is moved for healing.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Sometimes they are formed in the month I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or up to XV, and are entirely shaped like a child according to the measure of the wise sage, and it is necessary that the bailiff oversees all this, for perhaps similar things may happen.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	do as is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman of a dead child in her womb, as I said in the division, and there is no natural expulsion, and you are constrained to work with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	you must know if the woman is in good health and has no condition that causes fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary that the woman lie on her back, and let her knees incline downward, and raise her legs;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the attendant should hold her in two parts, so that she is positioned on the bed such that she is not inclined towards the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth with a paste of moist oil mixed with muscillega of horehound and fenugreek and flax seeds, then anoint her hands with these oils and these pastes;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	then gently press them into the paste lightly, then check one side where she presses to ensure they are suitable for her, and watch if the child is prepared to descend head first;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	Insert the hooks in his eyes or on his neck or in his mouth or at the back of his throat or behind his beard or in his armpit or near his ribs, and if the descent is on the legs, insert them in his toes and on the middle sides of his ribs;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he must hold the hook in his right hand, place the curve between his two fingers of his left hand, and press it gently with his whole hand, and insert the hook into any of those places we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the hook:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert the other hook opposite it, or a third one if needed, so that the extraction is even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stretch it evenly by moving from one side to the other, to allow movement out, and let the bandages be toothed to hold the movements, as shown in this figure:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if one part remains, anoint the side with some of his oils, and place it in that part, and pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if any remains, place this bandage higher up, and do so until it all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes in front of the other, and he cannot pull back for grasping, then you must wrap it up with a cloth until it all comes out;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then place it at the joint of the sole or heel, and thus you must do the same with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the head of the child is large and it is narrow at the birth canal, or there is an accumulation of fluid in the head, then you must insert a spatula between your two hands, cut the head, and extract the fluid;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	where you should round it with the instrument called "almidach," of which the shape comes with the instruments in the chapter that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and do the same if the child has a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then draw the bones with pliers, and if the head jumps forward and is tight against the forehead, cut through until the moisture that is in the foot passage is released;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if she cannot come out, cut her piece by piece until you can.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if he is swollen in the belly or between the ribs, you must pierce him until the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is on its feet, then the traction is light, and the adjustment to the mouth of the socket is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if he is tight in the belly or breast, you must dilate him with the finger wrapped in cloth;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and cut into the belly or breast until the moisture that is inside flows out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limbs are removed and the head remains, push your hand in through a hole perfectly in the flesh, and pull it out to the mouth of the wound;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then insert the needle at point one or two, and pull it through forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the wound is narrowed due to a hot abscess that has come upon it, one should not work on it, but rather administer moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the physician applies plasters, and slices in aqueous softening and moistening substances.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can make it level, then treat it as we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one has no power to do so, then pull it through in pieces, and leave nothing of the second skin.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, apply the treatment we mentioned for large abscesses that occur in the flesh;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, apply cold compresses, and use other treatments as necessary.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whom the fetus in her womb had died, then another was conceived afterwards, and that one too was stillborn.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she developed an abscess in her breast, which swelled so much that it burst, and began to fester severely.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat it, and I thought for a long time, and could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied an adhesive plaster, and out came a bone, and after several days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very amazed, because there are no bones in the abdomen.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that they were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I treated the wound, and manipulated the bones until the woman was in better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and treated the woman for a long time in this way, and she would then excrete a little pus from the area;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have recorded this chapter for the reason that when masters encounter something unusual, they know to seek help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to return the joint to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here follows the form of the cautery, as described in the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And to the two sides of the two shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be finer than the retort, and made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the tube should be two fingers wide, and the margin of the trees one finger, and its length half a palm;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two shoulders there should be two fittings of the same tube, which are firmly attached to each one, half a palm long or a bit more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two fittings are positioned at the mouth of the apparatus to open when the two horns are turned.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the likeness of the tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have two supports for the two heads, as you see, one palm in length, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you wish to open the birth canal with the instrument, have the woman sit on a bed, her feet hanging down and her legs spread, then insert the two supports together into the birth canal, and hold the head of the instrument beneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the instrument just as you did with the tongs equally, according to how much you wish to open the birth canal, until the woman's face shows what she wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all mounted, and their kinds are multiplied;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	and when the physician has them prepared, the work is done more quickly, and they are more valuable to people in proportion to their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despise the instrument because you have not prepared it, for their needs are not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second child is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze with condiments, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if it helps because of this, so be it.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take some honey and make a hole in the cover, then put herbs that can open the mouth of the mare, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cistus, and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or some of them, should be boiled in water over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then place one end of a tube in the opening of the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the mare, and hold it so that the vapor comes inside the mare;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	The second joint jumps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment and does not improve, instruct the bailiff to moisten his left hand in oil of sesame or in mallow decoction, and then place it on her body, and seek the second remedy;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when he has found it, take and stretch it little by little straightly, so that the mare does not fall during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but you must move it gently to the right and to the left, and then pull;
si venra et se desaerdra.	it will come and disengage.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the nostril is narrow and constricted, we have mentioned the treatment of sneezing, and of fumigating with herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it does not respond to all of what we have said, then be careful not to pull too forcefully;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary to tie the affected part of the nostril to the woman's thigh, then administer an enema of tetrapharmacum ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	it will relieve and reset, and it will come back to its place;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	however, when it reaches such a point that it causes bad odors in the stomach and head, and troubles the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Then appropriate fumigations should be used for them:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument used to fumigate the woman for retaining her flowers and secondine is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is similar to glass in appearance, and one places the head subtly in the nature, and the cheeks wide over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the fumigation be over the coals, and continue it until it is spent, and then start another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have a discernible anus, instead it is sealed by a fine membrane:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the surgeon to incise that suture at its proper place, and not with a sharp spatula, and guard against touching it.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place damp wool in wine and oil, then treat with ointment until he is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that he will keep it still, place a chain through the ring, and leave his hands bound for a day, and remove it when the child wishes to go to chambers.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this obstruction comes from the sudden closure of a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	it is necessary to cut that closure:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it should be treated, as we have said about the tendon of the thumb.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from inside the anus are nodular, and those that come near the anus or in the space between the two parts often have one fistula or multiple.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that knotting is old, it must be treated, and hot moist poultices or fine powders are applied, and sometimes these fistulas persist.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are recognized by the fact that there is vomiting or flatulence when the patient vomits, and sometimes worms come out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And there are fistulas that penetrate to the bladder, and to half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and extend to the joint of the thigh, and to the root of the kidney.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula penetrating to the fundament, and not penetrating:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And it is that you place your thumb at the base, and insert a fine needle of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no curvature.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is curvature, insert a fine thread of linen or horsehair until you feel the thread or hair with your thumb;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge or swelling or sign of life, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	you know that it does not penetrate;
si te haste dou curer.	so hurry to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula reaches to the bladder or to the conduit of urine, then urination occurs, and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it penetrates up to the knee joint, then the thread comes out at that location;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the cause of the pain is around it, then it will quickly become a bone deformity, and neither medicine nor speedy remedy by ointment will help;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persistent fistulas there is no cure other than work, and the vanity of foolish doctors who intervene in them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the case that is not persistent and is not old, there is hope for healing by iron, as I have experienced, and it is so that the patient lies on your lap on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and lift the legs up to the thighs, and keep the thighs inclined toward the abdomen;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	then insert a tent of linen, or of lead if there is twisting, until you know where the tent reaches.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around the fundament, then you must place your index finger there; if you then feel that the testicle has been pierced;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and if you feel the hole or flesh where your finger is, then you know it is pierced;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	do not attempt to treat it if it cannot be healed.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that some can be treated well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the treatment involves heating the cautery slightly according to the width of the fistula, as was mentioned before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and inserting it fully heated into the fistula until it reaches near the fundament;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times until you know that the burnt flesh is charred, which looks like a feather of a bird;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with cloths moistened with butter until the flesh grows back, then treat it with an ointment that promotes flesh growth and healing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healthy, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if the abscess enters but does not penetrate to the root which is at the base, and there is a thick layer of flesh or fat between your bone and the abscess, and you see the fistula under this layer of flesh;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	cut it from the beginning of the fistula and then proceed forward to the abscess, and afterwards apply the cautery until you reach the head of the abscess;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and the swelling will subside, and it will fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then clean the damaged tissues that look like a bird's feather, and leave nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood fails you, and cuts between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or with astringent medication.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery combines two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the cutting away of adhered tissues, and stopping the blood and drying the moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then treat moist swellings with butter or crushed substances, until the area weeps clear fluid, and remove the burned tissue from the wound.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then treat the wound with hardening ointments that adhere to the flesh, and the medications will dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes up from the depths of the fundament, and is distant from the body, then pierce it at the fundament, and examine it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and it is between II (the membrane or flesh), where it is near piercing, there should be no other way but one of faith and hope, by means of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it down to the base, or if possible place tents and treat it as described first;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, so as not to cut the tissue that holds the foundation, and induce vomiting as desired;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance it may heal, or remove that covering and clean it after it is cut near the base, either by tenting or with another appropriate instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then cleanse the wounded flesh in the wound as much as you can.
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound and to prevent a fistula outside the fundament:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	it will be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and it is when you insert the probe into the fistula, and it is near the fundament on the skin above, then take a probe with a point in this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And insert the thread twisted into two parts, and insert the probe along the entire length of the thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is perforated at the margin of the fundament inside, then extract the thread from that perforation, so you insert your finger into the fundament;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and join the two shoulders together, and hold them to each other, and leave it for one day or two;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it several times until the thread cuts through the tissues between them, and they come together;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, pierce it in all ways that you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not appropriate to make an incision too deep for the displacement and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spinous process where one makes the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is not, so that one does not cut what should not be cut, as you see here:
des emorroydes	for hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Emorrhoids occur in two manners:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	where they are inside the fundament, like seeds of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in the skin there is blood, and there may be one or more, and they are away from the fundament and at the head of the fundament;
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	but those that are away have little moisture, and often there is a small amount of yellowish water or a bit of blood, and they have the color of the flesh;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	and the treatment for those who have them inside the fundament is to instruct the patient to abstain from going out until the fundament feels better, and the children are aware;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	hurry and grasp it with forceps, holding it with your nail, then cut it at its root;
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if the hooks cannot hold because of moisture, they take them with a sponge, or cloth, or a piece of cotton;
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	and extract them with your hands, then cut them, and put on some hot powders that are used for cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the excrement cannot come out, give the patient a harsh and bitter enema to cleanse what is in the rectum so that it can pass freely;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient is constipated, and if the stool is hard in the rectum, then the treatment is easy;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And take them by your fingernail or with pincers, cut them off, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and that he fears the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary that you manage the suturing according to this method:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take the thread and tie it to a needle, then pull the thread from above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and twist the two ends of the thread under the needle, and let it be loose;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and tightly pull the thread, then tie the thread, and remove the needle, and do this for all of them, and leave one to allow the excess blood to flow;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place a damp strip of rose oil or cerate on the foundation, and place it on the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then leave them until they fall off, and when they have fallen off, treat them with ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from the dryness of the bowels or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is dryness of feces in the intestines, and by compulsion of nature, and when the illness is old and medicine does not avail.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	It is necessary that you cut with the tip of a spatula or your nail through the skin above it, without leaving it to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	then treat it until it is healed as necessary;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	and if it does not heal, then resume the shaving more vigorously than before until it heals well, even if it becomes chafed;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat until he is healed.
dou fremit	with trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	The flea is a small striped appearance on the body, and moves very quickly through it;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it is found in cold places, and one feels it like being chilled to the bone, and it spreads throughout the body, more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a quill from a goose feather or a strong eagle feather, and place the quill on the chill, until the circles around the chill completely enclose it;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then move your hand along the entire quill until you cover all around the chill, and place it quickly, and remove the chill from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, do this with a thread of linen or iron according to this form, and let it be fine underneath and drawn over:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce, to keep the hair on the head, and press the hair.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you wish, cauterize the tremor as it is before in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes a enema of silver or sorrel, or of melted silk or bran is made;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	and sometimes one uses small and large instruments, according to those to whom they are applied.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those who are treated in the care of children and those who are weak and in pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the enema, small and large, is as follows, or the belly is bandaged in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	and there should be a separation where the abdomen is bound as you see, and the intestines inside are perforated;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and there should be two holes on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the pouch where medicines are placed be made from a bladder of an animal or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and have one digit of space between each hole, then insert into these holes strong rawhide threads twisted ten times around, and assemble the pouch as if it were a drum.
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then administer as an enema;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the tip of the enema with oil or beaten egg white, or something similar, then insert it gently;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister presses the patient with both hands, until he is completely covered, then removes the enema, and lifts the patient's legs against the wall, and if the medicine wants to come out, let it flow as much as possible;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps one full night, then there is greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you give him an enema in a disease of diarrhea, and the medicine comes out too quickly, then repeat it until he is well.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are at the fundament, or an abscess, then the enema should be as fine as for a child;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the fine enema in which the skin is stretched:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already mentioned in the section the treatment of wounds;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Then we shall tell you about the remedies of hands and medicine, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds vary according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and from what they are made.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are due to the impact of stones, and the cutting of swords and knives, or spears or staffs or arrows, or similar objects;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or they are made according to the places on the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, or on the head, or on the foot, or on the belly, or on the liver, and similar parts;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because the memory of them will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound occurs on the head, and the bone is not broken, be careful whether it is from the impact of a stone or similar objects, and the skin is completely torn and the wound is large, and you fear the formation of a hot abscess:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	If you treat it immediately to staunch the bleeding from the head if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the dressing be on the opposite side of the injured part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and avoid having the patient become bloated from wine and heavy meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not wish to stop the bleeding, then let his meat diet be reduced, and he should not drink wine nor eat meat.
